##
#
#2400520 - Automatic Independent State init. Will fire if country revolted, released by player, OR by event. Will clear any puppet effects if they exist (2400530) and will also trigger forced peace (2400602) if legitIndie is not set.
#2400521 - Automatic Lvl1puppet Puppet init. Will fire if country is puppeted and puppetLevel1 flag is set, but not puppetLevel1made. Only triggers 2400531. Will ALSO fire if no puppetLevel flag is set at all,
#2400522 - Automatic Lvl2puppet Puppet init. Will fire if country is puppeted and puppetLevel2 flag is set, but not puppetLevel2made. Only triggers 2400532.
#2400523 - Automatic Lvl3puppet Puppet init. Will fire if country is puppeted and puppetLevel3 flag is set, but not puppetLevel3made. Only triggers 2400533.
#2400524 - Automatic Lvl4puppet Puppet init. Will fire if country is puppeted and puppetLevel4 flag is set, but not puppetLevel4made. Only triggers 2400534.
#2400525 - Automatic Lvl5puppet Puppet init. Will fire if country is puppeted and puppetLevel5 flag is set, but not puppetLevel5made. Only triggers 2400535.
#2400526 - Automatic Lvl6puppet Puppet init. Will fire if country is puppeted and puppetLevel6 flag is set, but not puppetLevel6made. Only triggers 2400536.
#2400527 - Automatic Lvl7puppet Puppet init. Will fire if country is puppeted and puppetLevel7 flag is set, but not puppetLevel7made. Only triggers 2400537.
#2400528 - Automatic Lvl8puppet Puppet init. Will fire if country is puppeted and puppetLevel8 flag is set, but not puppetLevel8made. Only triggers 2400538.
#2400529 - Automatic Lvl9puppet Puppet init. Will fire if country is puppeted and puppetLevel9 flag is set, but not puppetLevel9made. Only triggers 2400539.
#
#2400530 - Establishing Independent State. Can be triggered externally or by automatic 2400520. Will remove all other effects and switch the effects and flags to legitIndie.
#2400531 - Establishing Lvl1puppet Puppet. Can be triggered externally or by automatic 2400521. Will remove all other effects and switch the effects and flags to puppetLevel1.
#2400532 - Establishing Lvl2puppet Puppet. Can be triggered externally or by automatic 2400522. Will remove all other effects and switch the effects and flags to puppetLevel2.
#2400533 - Establishing Lvl3puppet Puppet. Can be triggered externally or by automatic 2400523. Will remove all other effects and switch the effects and flags to puppetLevel3.
#2400534 - Establishing Lvl4puppet Puppet. Can be triggered externally or by automatic 2400524. Will remove all other effects and switch the effects and flags to puppetLevel4.
#2400535 - Establishing Lvl5puppet Puppet. Can be triggered externally or by automatic 2400525. Will remove all other effects and switch the effects and flags to puppetLevel5.
#2400536 - Establishing Lvl6puppet Puppet. Can be triggered externally or by automatic 2400526. Will remove all other effects and switch the effects and flags to puppetLevel6.
#2400537 - Establishing Lvl7puppet Puppet. Can be triggered externally or by automatic 2400527. Will remove all other effects and switch the effects and flags to puppetLevel7.
#2400538 - Establishing Lvl8puppet Puppet. Can be triggered externally or by automatic 2400528. Will remove all other effects and switch the effects and flags to puppetLevel8.
#2400539 - Establishing Lvl9puppet Puppet. Can be triggered externally or by automatic 2400529. Will remove all other effects and switch the effects and flags to puppetLevel9.
#
#2400540 - IndpState	Dissent floor is zero
#2400541 - Lvl1puppet	Puppet Dissent floor. Will keep dissent at the minimum of 40% (effective 45%).
#2400542 - Lvl2puppet	Puppet Dissent floor. Will keep dissent at the minimum of 35% (effective 40%).
#2400543 - Lvl3puppet	Puppet Dissent floor. Will keep dissent at the minimum of 30% (effective 35%).
#2400544 - Lvl4puppet	Puppet Dissent floor. Will keep dissent at the minimum of 25% (effective 30%).
#2400545 - Lvl5puppet	Puppet Dissent floor. Will keep dissent at the minimum of 20% (effective 25%).
#2400546 - Lvl6puppet	Puppet Dissent floor. Will keep dissent at the minimum of 15% (effective 20%).
#2400547 - Lvl7puppet	Puppet Dissent floor. Will keep dissent at the minimum of 10% (effective 15%).
#2400548 - Lvl8puppet	Puppet Dissent floor. Will keep dissent at the minimum of  5% (effective 10%).
#2400549 - Lvl9puppet	Puppet Dissent floor. Will keep dissent at the minimum of  2% (effective  5%).
#
#2400550 - Adds    the counter-AI-cheat penalties. Will force AI to have the same IC penalties for dissent as human players.
#2400551 - Removes the counter-AI-cheat penalties. Will fire if formerly AI country becomes human controlled.
#2400552 - Setting the stayInWar flag to true. Country with the "stayInWar" flag will not quit the war if it ceases being a puppet.
#2400553 - Recording the puppet master
#
#2400600 - Resistance event chain starting point. Sets a timer to trigger 2400601 within a certain time period. 1 year for puppetLevel1, 2 years for puppetLevel2, 4 years for puppetLevel3
#2400601 - If still a puppet, one of 3 things will happen: revolution fails (5% dissent gain); 25% revolution succeeds (will end puppet status and trigger 2400530 & 2400602), 25% civil war (10% dissent and massive rebellions)
#2400602 - Break alliances, reset sliders, and set high neutrality. If still a puppet, will addcore on 2923 and trigger 2400603
#2400603 - The intervention - puppet goes to war with the former master
#2400604 - Widespread revolt - revolution fails but lots of rebels spawn instead
#2400605 - Trade relations reset. Useful for countries undergoing radical change i.e. sudden civil war.
##

event = {
	id = 2400520
	random = no 
	persistent = yes

	name = "A Sovereign State"
	desc = "Our government represents a fully independent and sovereign state. At least - it is largely perceived as such by the local population and the international community alike."
	style = 2
	
	trigger = { 
		local_flag = AllInit
		#NOT = { local_flag = indiePrep }
		NOT = { ispuppet = yes }
		OR = {
			NOT = { local_flag = legitIndie }
			local_flag = puppetLevel1made
			local_flag = puppetLevel2made
			local_flag = puppetLevel3made
			local_flag = puppetLevel4made
			local_flag = puppetLevel5made
			local_flag = puppetLevel6made
			local_flag = puppetLevel7made
			local_flag = puppetLevel8made
			local_flag = puppetLevel9made
		}
	}
	
	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1913 }
	offset = 3
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action = {
		name = "We are creating a better future"
		command = { type = trigger which = 2400530 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = legitIndie } NOT = { local_flag = stayInWar } local_flag = puppetOf } type = trigger which = 2400602 } #former puppet turns on master
	}
}

event = {
	id = 2400521
	random = no 
	persistent = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		#local_flag = indiePrep
		NOT = { local_flag = puppetLevel1made }
		
		#Is default
		OR = {
			local_flag = puppetLevel1
			NOT = {
				local_flag = puppetLevel1
				local_flag = puppetLevel2
				local_flag = puppetLevel3
				local_flag = puppetLevel4
				local_flag = puppetLevel5
				local_flag = puppetLevel6
				local_flag = puppetLevel7
				local_flag = puppetLevel8
				local_flag = puppetLevel9
			}
		}

		ispuppet = yes
	}

	name = "The Puppet State (weakest)"
	desc = "This government has been established by an occupying power to give its presense a semblance of legalitate rule. It lacks any domestic and international legitimacy, it is distrusted by the overwhelming majority of the population and challanged by a host of very powerful resistance organizations - 'the underground state'. De-facto, this is a government of foreign occupation, with no real domestic support."
	style = 2	
	
	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1913 }
	offset = 10
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action = {
		name = "We are creating a better future."
		command = { type = trigger which = 2400531 }
	}
}

		NOT = { local_flag = joinAlliance }

		war = { country = GER }
		war = { country = ENG country = GER }
		NOT = { participant = { value = 4 } }
		NOT = { country = USA }
	}

	name = "Joining the Allies"
	desc = "We are at war with Germany. Is it time to join the Allies?"
	style = 2	
	
	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1913 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action = {
		name = "Join the Allies!"
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = local_setflag which = joinAlliance }
		command = { type = alliance which = ENG }
	}
	action = {
		name = "Chart our own way"
		ai_chance = 0
		command = { type = local_setflag which = joinAlliance }
	}
}
